reaction_dwarf_civ

[OBJECT:REACTION]

New vanilla workshop additions first.Then modded entries.

[REACTION:PROCESS_MILK]
      [NAME:Pasteurize milk]
	  [DESCRIPTION:Takes a bucket of milk and makes it safe to drink, clearing it from bacteria. It fills the milk in a barrel, allowing your units to drink it. Costs 1 fuel for heating.]
      [BUILDING:KITCHEN:CUSTOM_P]
      [REAGENT:A:150:LIQUID_MISC:NONE:NONE:NONE]
         [REACTION_CLASS:MILK]
         [UNROTTEN]
      [REAGENT:B:1:NONE:NONE:NONE:NONE][CONTAINS:A][PRESERVE_REAGENT][DOES_NOT_DETERMINE_PRODUCT_AMOUNT]
      [REAGENT:C:1:NONE:NONE:NONE:NONE][EMPTY][FOOD_STORAGE_CONTAINER][PRESERVE_REAGENT][DOES_NOT_DETERMINE_PRODUCT_AMOUNT]
      [PRODUCT:100:5:DRINK:NONE:GET_MATERIAL_FROM_REAGENT:A:NONE][PRODUCT_DIMENSION:150][PRODUCT_TO_CONTAINER:C] => 1.
      [SKILL:COOK][FUEL]

[REACTION:MAKE_CRYSTAL_ROCK]
[NAME:Smelt sand and lead into rough rock crystals.]
[DESCRIPTION:Takes a bar of lead and a bag of sand to create three rough rock crystals.]
[DESCRIPTION:]
[DESCRIPTION:Uses smelting skill.]
[BUILDING:SMELTER:CUSTOM_SHIFT_R]
[REAGENT:A:150:BAR:NONE:INORGANIC:LEAD]
	[REAGENT:sand:150:POWDER_MISC:NONE:NONE:NONE]
		[IS_SAND_MATERIAL] 
	[REAGENT:sand container:1:NONE:NONE:NONE:NONE]
		[CONTAINS:sand]
		[PRESERVE_REAGENT]
		[DOES_NOT_DETERMINE_PRODUCT_AMOUNT]
	[PRODUCT:100:3:ROUGH:NONE:INORGANIC:CRYSTAL_ROCK]
	[SKILL:SMELT]
	

[REACTION:MAKE_INK_FROM_ASH]
[NAME:Cook ash into ink]
[DESCRIPTION:Takes a bar of ash and an empty pot and create 5 units of ink. Ink is used in the scriptorium to write books.]
[DESCRIPTION:]
[DESCRIPTION:Uses cooking skill.]
[BUILDING:KITCHEN:CUSTOM_I]
[REAGENT:A:150:BAR:NONE:ASH:NONE]
[REAGENT:B:1:TOOL:ITEM_TOOL_LARGE_POT:NONE:NONE]
	[PRESERVE_REAGENT][EMPTY]
	[DOES_NOT_DETERMINE_PRODUCT_AMOUNT]
[PRODUCT:100:5:LIQUID_MISC:NONE:INORGANIC:INK][PRODUCT_DIMENSION:150][PRODUCT_TO_CONTAINER:B]
	[SKILL:COOK]
	


[REACTION:LUA_HOOK_USEWATER_WATERWELL_BUCKET]
	[NAME:Fill a bucket with water(7)]
[DESCRIPTION:Takes an empty bucket and fills it with water. Handpump must be build near water, for example next to a river or pond.]
[DESCRIPTION:]
[DESCRIPTION:Uses pump-operator skill.]
	[BUILDING:HANDPUMP:CUSTOM_A]
	[REAGENT:A:1:BUCKET:NONE:NONE:NONE][PRESERVE_REAGENT] [EMPTY]
	[PRODUCT:100:7:LIQUID_MISC:NONE:WATER:NONE][PRODUCT_TO_CONTAINER:A]
	[PRODUCT_DIMENSION:150]
	[SKILL:OPERATE_PUMP]

[REACTION:LUA_HOOK_USEWATER_WATERWELL_BARREL]
	[NAME:Fill a barrel with water(10)]
[DESCRIPTION:Takes an empty barrel and fills it with water. The water barrel will count as drink and units drink from it. Handpump must be build near water, for example next to a river or pond.]
[DESCRIPTION:]
[DESCRIPTION:Uses pump-operator skill.]
	[BUILDING:HANDPUMP:CUSTOM_B]
	[REAGENT:barrel:1:BARREL:NONE:NONE:NONE]
		[EMPTY]
		[FOOD_STORAGE_CONTAINER]
		[PRESERVE_REAGENT]
		[DOES_NOT_DETERMINE_PRODUCT_AMOUNT]
	[PRODUCT:100:10:DRINK:NONE:WATER:NONE][PRODUCT_TO_CONTAINER:barrel]
	[PRODUCT_DIMENSION:150]
	[SKILL:OPERATE_PUMP]

### splitting crafts/large gems ###

[REACTION:GEM_SPLIT_GEM]
   [NAME:Split Large Gem into 3 gems]
[DESCRIPTION:Takes a large gem and creates three small gems of the same type.]
[DESCRIPTION:]
[DESCRIPTION:Uses gemcutting skill.]
   [BUILDING:GEMCUTTER:CUSTOM_ALT_A]
   [BUILDING:GUILD_JEWELER_N:CUSTOM_ALT_A]
   [REAGENT:A:1:GEM:NO_SUBTYPE:INORGANIC:NONE][REACTION_CLASS:GEM]
   [PRODUCT:100:3:SMALLGEM:NONE:GET_MATERIAL_FROM_REAGENT:A:NONE]

	[SKILL:CUTGEM]

[REACTION:COPY_WEAPON_GOLD]
[NAME:Copy golden weapon]
[BUILDING:INVENTOR:CUSTOM_W]
[BUILDING:GUILD_HEALER_W:CUSTOM_W]
[DESCRIPTION:Takes a weapon and 5 metal bars to make a copy of it. Uses Weaponsmith skill.]
[CATEGORY:GOLD_COPY]
[CATEGORY_NAME:Copy golden items]
[CATEGORY_DESCRIPTION:Copy items made of gold; intended to reverse-engineer looted weapons and armors from invaders.]
[CATEGORY_KEY:CUSTOM_G]
[REAGENT:A:750:BAR:NONE:INORGANIC:GOLD]
[REAGENT:B:1:WEAPON:NONE:INORGANIC:GOLD]
	[PRESERVE_REAGENT]
	[DOES_NOT_DETERMINE_PRODUCT_AMOUNT]
[PRODUCT:100:1:GET_ITEM_DATA_FROM_REAGENT:B:NONE]
			[SKILL:FORGE_WEAPON]

runesmith


[REACTION:SPATTER_ADD_AMMO_ADAMANTINE]
	[NAME:Engrave adamantine runes (double damage)] 
	[BUILDING:RUNESMITH:CUSTOM_A][BUILDING:RUNESMITH:CUSTOM_A]
	[DESCRIPTION:Causing the enemy to take double damage by any weapon on hit.]
	[DESCRIPTION:Uses Engraving skill.]
[CATEGORY:AMMO_RUNE]
[CATEGORY_NAME:Engrave ammo with runes]
[CATEGORY_DESCRIPTION:Takes a stack of ammo and engraves it with powerful runes adding special effects to attacks. The effect depends on the metal used for the runes.]
[CATEGORY_KEY:CUSTOM_A]
	[REAGENT:A:150:BAR:NONE:NONE:NONE]
		[REACTION_CLASS:ADAMANTINE_COATING]
	[REAGENT:object:5:AMMO:NONE:NONE:NONE][PRESERVE_REAGENT]
	[IMPROVEMENT:800:object:COVERED:INORGANIC:ADAMANTINE_COATING]
	[SKILL:DETAILSTONE] was soapmaker/runesmith[FUEL]

[REACTION:SPATTER_ADD_TRAP_ADAMANTINE]
	[NAME:Engrave adamantine runes (double damage)]
	[BUILDING:RUNESMITH:CUSTOM_SHIFT_A][BUILDING:RUNESMITH:CUSTOM_SHIFT_A]
	[DESCRIPTION:Causing the enemy to take double damage by any weapon on hit.]
[CATEGORY:TRAP_RUNE]
[CATEGORY_NAME:Engrave trap with runes]
[CATEGORY_DESCRIPTION:Takes a trap component and engraves it with powerful runes adding special effects to attacks. The effect depends on the metal used for the runes.]
[CATEGORY_KEY:CUSTOM_T]
[REAGENT:A:150:BAR:NONE:NONE:NONE]
		[REACTION_CLASS:ADAMANTINE_COATING]
	[REAGENT:object:1:TRAPCOMP:NONE:NONE:NONE][PRESERVE_REAGENT]
	[IMPROVEMENT:800:object:COVERED:INORGANIC:ADAMANTINE_COATING]
